    45	## What Was Built
    46	
    47	**Implemented + tested (2026-05-30).** All five families of the single-writer/durability cluster landed as one coordinated change set, each finding re-validated at HEAD by symbol and covered by a deterministic regression test:
    48	
    49	- **Family 1+2 — `model-server-supervision.cjs`**: respawn-lock staleness now bounded by listener liveness (DR-005); the lazy demand listener re-arms on a failed spawn (DR-006); idle eviction reaps the root process, not just descendants (DR-012).
    50	- **Family 4 durability — `vector-index-store.ts`**: the clean-shutdown marker is deleted only after a confirmed-successful close (DR-011).
    51	- **Family 4 durability — `reindex.ts`**: same-dimension reindex writes a staging shard and atomic-swaps on success; the worker re-reads the cancel flag mid-run (DR-020 + DR-001-P1-002).
    52	- **Family 4 perimeter — `hf-model-server.cjs`**: the direct-startup unlink path applies the ownership/live-resident perimeter guard, and tcp targets enforce loopback/auth (DR-001-P2-001 + DR-002-P1-001).
    53	- **Family 3 leases — `daemon-detect.ts`**: a stale-looking launcher lease with a live recorded `childPid` is no longer treated as reclaimable (DR-016). OR-R-01 was re-validated as already O_EXCL-remediated at HEAD — no change.
    54

    71	## How It Was Delivered
    72	
    73	A multi-agent design pass produced the coordinated plan; it was then re-validated against HEAD-read source (correcting the OR-R-01 already-done and DR-012 mechanism items) and cross-checked against `031/review/review-report.md`. The plan was captured as this committed packet so the work is durable and ready to execute as one careful effort — exactly as the handover mandates (one coordinated packet, after the launcher-WIP precondition gate, with a deterministic two-launcher concurrency test). Implementation was intentionally NOT attempted at the tail of a long session because this is the highest-blast-radius surface in the repo (the program exists because of a DB-corruption incident here) and the design itself requires per-finding HEAD re-validation plus a gate.

    79	## Key Decisions
    80	
    81	| Decision | Why |
    82	|----------|-----|
    83	| Design first as a committed packet, then implement | The ready plan was captured durably so the implementation could be re-validated against it per family rather than rushed |
    84	| Implement as one coordinated change set per family | The findings share a respawn lock / root-liveness authority / leases / marker; piecemeal fixes re-collide (handover mandate) |
    85	| Honor the precondition gate before Family-3 | The code-graph launcher is adjacent-session territory; OR-R-01 is already remediated |
    86	| Deterministic Harness A/B, no real sleeps | Concurrency bugs need reproducible RED-before / GREEN-after evidence via injected time/liveness/spawn |

   108	<!-- ANCHOR:limitations -->
   109	## Known Limitations
   110	
   111	1. **Concurrency tests are deterministic, not live.** Harness A/B inject `nowMs`/`liveness`/`spawnFn`/`signal` to force races without real sleeps. A live two-launcher integration run (real processes) remains gated on a working `onnxruntime` tree, as documented in packet 005 — these unit-level suites assert the corrected logic, not end-to-end residency.
   112	2. **Family-3 scope.** DR-016 was fixed in `daemon-detect.ts` (this skill's territory); OR-R-01 was only re-validated (already O_EXCL in the code-graph launcher, adjacent-session territory — untouched).
   113	3. **`reindex.ts` cluster fix sits alongside the C2 cancel edit** (packet 008); both were re-validated together so the staging-swap and cancel-re-read are consistent.

     1	---
     2	title: "407 — Adversarial near-miss (lexical overlap, semantic distance)"
     3	description: "Fire a query whose stem overlaps lexically with multiple corpus files but is semantically distant from most of them. Verify the semantically-correct file outranks the lexical decoys."
     4	audited_post_018: true
     5	---
     6	
     7	# 407 — Adversarial near-miss (lexical overlap, semantic distance)
     8	
     9	## 1. OVERVIEW
    10	
    11	A lexical-only ranker (FTS5, BM25) would rank by term-frequency overlap; a semantic ranker should weight meaning. This scenario fires queries crafted so that the lexically-closest file is semantically WRONG, and the semantically-correct file has lower term overlap.
    12	
    13	If BGE local fallback's semantic representation is functioning correctly, it pulls the right answer despite lexical decoys. If it's degraded (or the embedding lane is disabled in favor of FTS5), the wrong file ranks first.
    14	
    15	---
    16	
    17	## 2. SCENARIO CONTRACT
    18	
    19	- Objective: Confirm semantic > lexical when they disagree.
    20	- Real user request: `Verify Code Graph's semantic ranking beats lexical decoys: fire 3 adversarial queries and confirm the semantically-correct file ranks above the lexical decoy in each top-5.`
    21	- RCAF Prompt: `As a query-intelligence validation operator, fire 3 adversarial queries with intentional lexical decoys and verify the semantically-correct file outranks the decoy in each top-5. Return a pass/fail verdict.`
    22	- Expected execution process: run 3 queries with engineered lexical+semantic mismatch, identify the correct file and the decoy in each result list, check ranks.
    23	- Expected signals: correct file rank < decoy rank in ≥ 2 of 3 queries.
    24	- Desired user-visible outcome: `PASS — semantic ranking beats lexical decoy in 3/3 queries.`
    25	- Pass/fail: PASS if 3/3; PARTIAL if 2/3; FAIL if ≤ 1.
    26	
    27	---
    28	
    29	## 3. TEST EXECUTION
    30	
    31	### Prompt
    32	
    33	```
    34	Fire 3 adversarial queries with engineered lexical decoys; confirm semantic ranking wins.
    35	```
    36	
    37	### Commands
    38	
    39	**Query A — "embedding cache" decoy:**
    40	Lexical decoy: `embedding-circuit-breaker.vitest.ts` (high term overlap with "embedding")
    41	Semantic target: `mcp_server/lib/cache/embedding-cache.ts` (the actual cache impl)
    42	
    43	```
    44	mcp__mk_code_index__code_graph_query({
    45	  query: "where are embedding results cached by content hash to skip recomputation",
    46	  num_results: 10,
    47	})
    48	```
    49	
    50	Confirm: `embedding-cache.ts` ranks above `embedding-circuit-breaker.vitest.ts`.
    51	
    52	**Query B — "vector store" decoy:**
    53	Lexical decoy: `vector-index-impl.vitest.ts` (test file)
    54	Semantic target: `mcp_server/lib/search/vector-index-store.ts` (the impl)
    55	
    56	```
    57	mcp__mk_code_index__code_graph_query({
    58	  query: "core class that opens the sqlite-vec virtual table for runtime vector queries",
    59	  num_results: 10,
    60	})
    61	```
    62	
    63	Confirm: `vector-index-store.ts` ranks above `vector-index-impl.vitest.ts`.
    64	
    65	**Query C — "provider factory" decoy:**
    66	Lexical decoy: `embeddings-ollama-factory.vitest.ts` (test file)
    67	Semantic target: `shared/embeddings/factory.ts` (the impl)
    68	
    69	```
    70	mcp__mk_code_index__code_graph_query({
    71	  query: "primary entry point that constructs concrete embedding provider instances and resolves auto cascade",
    72	  num_results: 10,
    73	})
    74	```
    75	
    76	Confirm: `factory.ts` ranks above `embeddings-ollama-factory.vitest.ts`.
    77	
    78	For each query, capture:
    79	- Rank of the semantic target.
    80	- Rank of the lexical decoy.
    81	- Boolean: target ranked above decoy?
    82	
    83	### Expected
    84	
    85	```
    86	| Query | Semantic target              | Target rank | Lexical decoy                   | Decoy rank | Target > Decoy? |
    87	|-------|------------------------------|------------:|---------------------------------|-----------:|----------------|
    88	| A     | embedding-cache.ts           | 1           | embedding-circuit-breaker.vitest| 6          | YES            |
    89	| B     | vector-index-store.ts        | 2           | vector-index-impl.vitest.ts     | 5          | YES            |
    90	| C     | factory.ts                   | 1           | embeddings-ollama-factory.vt | 4          | YES            |
    91	```
    92	
    93	### Evidence
    94	
    95	- The 3 queries verbatim.
    96	- The top-10 result paths for each.
    97	- The rank-pair table.
    98	- An honest note: if the decoy ranks above the target, IS the decoy actually a better answer for this query? (Test files can sometimes be the most explicit single source for a behavior — that's a legitimate edge case, not a ranker failure.)
    99	- Active provider from memory_health.
   100	
   101	## 4. PASS PREDICATE
   102	
   103	A FAIL signal indicates one of:
   104	1. The embedding lane is degraded or disabled.
   105	2. The lexical (FTS5) score is being weighted too heavily in the hybrid-search composition.
   106	3. The corpus genuinely lacks an alternative to the decoy file (sparse-content issue, not a ranker issue).
   107	
   108	Differentiate (1)/(2) from (3) by inspecting the top-10 — if MANY test/decoy files cluster at the top and the impl is buried, it's (1)/(2). If the impl simply doesn't have rich content, it's (3) and the test is inconclusive.

.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/026-graph-and-context-optimization/007-mcp-daemon-reliability/014-infra-memory-db-and-graph-churn/implementation-summary.md:47:Two live-infra issues were root-caused. .opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/026-graph-and-context-optimization/007-mcp-daemon-reliability/014-infra-memory-db-and-graph-churn/implementation-summary.md:49:### Memory-DB `SQLITE_CONSTRAINT_PRIMARYKEY`
.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/026-graph-and-context-optimization/007-mcp-daemon-reliability/014-infra-memory-db-and-graph-churn/implementation-summary.md:50:Every memory write funnels through one `INSERT` into `memory_index`, which fires the FTS5 sync trigger `memory_fts_insert` (`INSERT INTO memory_fts(rowid,...) VALUES(new.id,...)`). The on-disk **FTS5 shadow** (`memory_fts_data`) is desynced/half-written from an unclean shutdown (a `.unclean-shutdown` marker is present), so the trigger's shadow insert hits a duplicate rowid → `SQLITE_CONSTRAINT_PRIMARYKEY`, aborting the whole `memory_index` insert. The boot integrity probe is detect-only and does not repair, so the corrupt shadow persists into every write. This is data-state corruption (matching a documented prior incident on this exact DB), not a logic defect. **Fix (operator-gated): rebuild the FTS shadow** — `INSERT INTO memory_fts(memory_fts) VALUES('rebuild')` then `('integrity-check')`, then VACUUM — via `memory_health autoRepair` or the FTS runbook, on a DB copy first. Touches only the derived index, not source rows.
.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/026-graph-and-context-optimization/007-mcp-daemon-reliability/014-infra-memory-db-and-graph-churn/implementation-summary.md:52:### Graph-metadata `last_save_at` churn (~634 files)
.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/026-graph-and-context-optimization/007-mcp-daemon-reliability/014-infra-memory-db-and-graph-churn/implementation-summary.md:53:The save path invokes the graph-metadata refresh with the **default root** (the whole `.opencode/specs` tree, including `z_archive/` and `z_future/`) instead of scoping to the saved folder, and writes `last_save_at` (a wall-clock `now()`) **unconditionally** — so every save rewrites the timestamp on all ~634 packets. **Fix (code): (1)** scope the save-time refresh to the touched folder; **(2)** write `last_save_at` only when the derived metadata actually changed (compare ignoring the timestamp); **(3)** exclude `z_archive`/`z_future` from the global walker and keep the repo-wide backfill as an explicit opt-in flag, not a save-time default.
.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/026-graph-and-context-optimization/007-mcp-daemon-reliability/014-infra-memory-db-and-graph-churn/implementation-summary.md:69:The two issues were investigated read-only by parallel agents and cross-checked against source + the documented prior corruption bug-report. Neither fix was applied: the memory-DB repair mutates a 1 GB live DB and is operator-gated (it belongs in `/doctor memory` / the runbook, with a DB-copy probe to choose the branch); and the graph-churn code fix touches operator-sensitive metadata-writing code (`graph-metadata-parser.ts`) at a time when the session's Read/shell tooling was degraded (mangled output, elided reads) — editing under those conditions would violate the READ-FIRST and HALT laws. One investigation agent exceeded its read-only brief and wrote an in-place idempotency guard into `graph-metadata-parser.ts`; that change was reverted to known-good HEAD and preserved at `/tmp/graph-metadata-parser.AGENT-PROPOSED.ts` as a reference to re-derive (not trust blindly) when the fix is applied.

.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/026-graph-and-context-optimization/007-mcp-daemon-reliability/014-infra-memory-db-and-graph-churn/implementation-summary.md:82:| Prefer FTS-rebuild over id-dedupe for the DB | Touches only the derived index; matches the documented prior fix; never `INSERT OR REPLACE` on `memory_index` (would cascade-delete FK children) |

   300	// Deferred indexing - entry searchable via BM25/FTS5 only
   301	/**
   302	 * Indexes a memory record without storing an embedding yet.
   303	 * @param params - The deferred memory values to index.
   304	 * @returns The indexed memory identifier.
   305	 */
   306	export function index_memory_deferred(
   307	  params: IndexMemoryDeferredParams,
   308	  database: Database.Database = initialize_db(),
   309	): number {
   310	  const {
   311	    specFolder,
   312	    filePath,
   313	    parentId = null,
   314	    anchorId = null,
   315	    title = null,
   316	    triggerPhrases = [],
   317	    importanceWeight = 0.5,
   318	    failureReason = null,
   319	    encodingIntent,
   320	    documentType = 'memory',
   321	    specLevel = null,
   322	    contentText = null,
   323	    qualityScore = 0,
   324	    qualityFlags = [],
   325	    appendOnly = false,
   326	  } = params;
   327	
   328	  const now = new Date().toISOString();
   329	  const triggers_json = JSON.stringify(triggerPhrases);
   330	  const canonicalFilePath = getCanonicalPathKey(filePath);
   331	
   332	  const stmts = init_prepared_statements(database);
   333	  const existing = appendOnly
   334	    ? null
   335	    : stmts.get_by_folder_and_path.get(specFolder, canonicalFilePath, filePath, anchorId, anchorId);
   336	
   337	  const index_memory_deferred_tx = database.transaction(() => {
   338	    if (existing && !appendOnly) {
   339	      database.prepare(`
   340	        UPDATE memory_index
   341	        SET title = ?,
   342	            trigger_phrases = ?,
   343	            importance_weight = ?,
   344	            canonical_file_path = ?,
   345	            embedding_status = 'pending',
   346	            failure_reason = ?,
   347	            updated_at = ?,
   348	            encoding_intent = COALESCE(?, encoding_intent),
   349	            document_type = ?,
   350	            spec_level = ?,
   351	            content_text = ?,
   352	            quality_score = ?,
   353	            quality_flags = ?,
   354	            retry_count = 0,
   355	            last_retry_at = NULL
   356	        WHERE id = ?
   357	      `).run(title, triggers_json, importanceWeight, canonicalFilePath, failureReason, now, encodingIntent, documentType, specLevel, contentText, qualityScore, JSON.stringify(qualityFlags), existing.id);
   358	      upsert_active_projection(database, specFolder, canonicalFilePath, anchorId, existing.id, now);
   359	      refresh_interference_scores_for_folder(database, specFolder);
   360	      return existing.id;
   361	    }
   362	
   363	    const result = database.prepare(`
   364	      INSERT INTO memory_index (
   365	        spec_folder, file_path, canonical_file_path, anchor_id, title, trigger_phrases,
   366	        importance_weight, created_at, updated_at, embedding_status,
   367	        failure_reason, retry_count, encoding_intent, document_type, spec_level,
   368	        content_text, quality_score, quality_flags, parent_id
   369	      ) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 'pending', ?, 0, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
   370	    `).run(
   371	      specFolder, filePath, canonicalFilePath, anchorId, title, triggers_json,
   372	      importanceWeight, now, now, failureReason, encodingIntent ?? 'document', documentType, specLevel, contentText, qualityScore, JSON.stringify(qualityFlags), parentId
   373	    );
   374	
   375	    const row_id = BigInt(result.lastInsertRowid);
   376	    upsert_active_projection(database, specFolder, canonicalFilePath, anchorId, Number(row_id), now);
   377	    refresh_interference_scores_for_folder(database, specFolder);
   378	    logger.info(`Deferred indexing: Memory ${Number(row_id)} saved without embedding (BM25/FTS5 searchable)`);
   379	
   380	    return Number(row_id);
   381	  });
   382	
   383	  return index_memory_deferred_tx();
   384	}

   720	    try {
   721	      fs.mkdirSync(lockDir);
   722	      return true;
   723	    } catch (error) {
   724	      if (error.code !== 'EEXIST') {
   725	        throw error;
   726	      }
   727	      // Reclaim a stale lockdir left by a SIGKILL'd launcher (mtime-based; the lockdir records no pid),
   728	      // so a crashed holder cannot block a requireLock respawn for the full 120s deadline.
   729	      try {
   730	        const ageMs = Date.now() - fs.statSync(lockDir).mtimeMs;
   731	        if (ageMs > BOOTSTRAP_LOCK_STALE_MS) {
   732	          log(`reclaiming stale bootstrap lock ${rel(lockDir)} (age ${Math.round(ageMs / 1000)}s)`);
   733	          fs.rmSync(lockDir, { recursive: true, force: true });
   734	          continue;
   735	        }
   736	      } catch (statErr) {
   737	        if (statErr.code === 'ENOENT') continue;
   738	        throw statErr;
   739	      }
   740	      if (artifactsReady() && !requireLock) {
   741	        return false;
   742	      }
   743	      if (Date.now() > deadline) {
   744	        throw new Error(`bootstrap lock timed out at ${rel(lockDir)}`);
   745	      }
   746	      await sleep(1000);
   747	    }
   748	  }
   749	}
   750	
   751	function launchServer() {
   752	  if (shouldSkipLaunch(childProcess)) {
   753	    log('launchServer skipped: a context-server child is already running in this launcher process');
   754	    return false;
   755	  }
   756	  if (!crashLoopGuard) crashLoopGuard = createCrashLoopGuard(getCrashLoopConfig());
   757	  if (supervisorRelaunchTimer) {
   758	    clearTimeout(supervisorRelaunchTimer);
   759	    supervisorRelaunchTimer = null;
   760	  }
   761	  const server = path.join(kitDir, 'mcp_server', 'dist', 'context-server.js');
   762	  const nodeArgs = getContextServerNodeArgs();
   763	  childProcess = spawn(process.execPath, [...nodeArgs, server], {
   764	    cwd: root,
   765	    env: process.env,
   766	    stdio: 'inherit',
   767	  });
   768	  const childPid = childProcess.pid;
   769	  writeLeaseFile(childPid);
   770	  startRssWatchdog(childPid);
   771	
   772	  childProcess.on('exit', (code, signal) => {
   773	    if (launcherShutdownInProgress) {
   774	      return;
   775	    }
   776	    const result = superviseChildExit(
   777	      { code, signal, childPid, intentional: false },
   778	      {
   779	        crashLoopGuard,
   780	        clearLease: clearLeaseFile,
   781	        reapProcessGroup: reapProcessTreeGroups,
   782	        mirrorSignal: (exitSignal) => process.kill(process.pid, exitSignal),
   783	        exit: (exitCode) => process.exit(exitCode),
   784	        scheduleRelaunch: (backoffMs) => {
   785	          log(`context-server child exited code=${code ?? 'null'} signal=${signal ?? 'null'}; relaunching in ${backoffMs}ms`);
   786	          supervisorRelaunchTimer = setTimeout(() => launchServer(), backoffMs);
   787	          supervisorRelaunchTimer.unref?.();
   788	        },
   789	      },
   790	    );
   791	    if (result.action === 'give-up') {
   792	      log(`context-server crash loop detected after ${result.deathsInWindow} deaths; clearing lease and mirroring child exit`);
   793	    }
   794	  });
   795	
   796	  childProcess.on('error', (error) => {
   797	    log(error.stack || error.message);
   798	    process.exit(1);
   799	  });
   800	  return true;
   801	}
   802	
   803	async function shutdownLauncherForSignal(signal) {
   804	  if (launcherShutdownInProgress) return;
   805	  launcherShutdownInProgress = true;
   806	  if (rssWatchdogTimer) clearInterval(rssWatchdogTimer);
   807	  if (supervisorRelaunchTimer) clearTimeout(supervisorRelaunchTimer);
   808	  hfControl.clearTimers();
   809	  await hfControl.stopDemandListener();
   810	
   811	  const children = [];
   812	  if (isChildRunning(childProcess)) {
   813	    children.push({ child: childProcess, label: 'context-server' });
   814	  }
   815	  const modelServerChild = hfControl.getChild();
   816	  if (isChildRunning(modelServerChild)) {
   817	    children.push({ child: modelServerChild, label: 'hf-model-server' });
   818	  }
   819	
   820	  if (children.length === 0) {
   821	    clearLeaseFile();
   822	    process.exit(128);
   823	    return;
   824	  }
   825	
   826	  for (const { child, label } of children) {
   827	    if (label === 'hf-model-server') {
   828	      hfControl.reapProcessTree(child.pid);
   829	    }
   830	    child.kill(signal);
   831	  }
   832	
   833	  const exited = await Promise.race([
   834	    Promise.all(children.map(({ child }) => waitForChildExit(child, RESPAWN_REAP_GRACE_MS))).then((results) => results.every(Boolean)),
   835	    sleep(RESPAWN_REAP_GRACE_MS).then(() => false),
   836	  ]);
   837	  if (!exited) {
   838	    for (const { child } of children) {
   839	      if (isChildRunning(child)) child.kill('SIGKILL');
   840	    }
   841	  }
   842	  clearLeaseFile();
   843	  process.exit(128);
   844	}
   845	
   846	function installSignalHandlers() {
   847	  for (const signal of ['SIGINT', 'SIGTERM', 'SIGHUP', 'SIGQUIT']) {
   848	    process.on(signal, () => {
   849	      void shutdownLauncherForSignal(signal).catch((error) => {
   850	        log(error.stack || error.message);
   851	        clearLeaseFile();
   852	        process.exit(128);
   853	      });
   854	    });
   855	  }
   856	  process.on('uncaughtException', (err) => {
   857	    try {
   858	      clearLeaseFile();
   859	    } catch {
   860	      // Preserve default uncaughtException crash behavior.
   861	    }
   862	    throw err;
   863	  });
   864	}
   865

   867	  loadProjectEnvFiles();
   868	  const started = now();
   869	  const actions = [];

   871

   890	    }

   894	    enforceStandaloneCodeGraphDb(actions);

   695	  connection: Database.Database,
   696	  target_path: string,
   697	  vec_available: boolean,
   698	): void {
   699	  const previousDb = db;
   700	  const previousPath = db_path;

   703	  sqlite_vec_available_flag = vec_available;

   732	function get_unclean_shutdown_marker_path(target_path: string): string | null {
   733	  if (target_path === ':memory:') {
   734	    return null;
   735	  }
   736	  return path.join(path.dirname(target_path), UNCLEAN_SHUTDOWN_MARKER);

   738	
   739	function write_unclean_shutdown_marker(target_path: string): void {
   740	  const marker_path = get_unclean_shutdown_marker_path(target_path);
   741	  if (!marker_path) {
   742	    return;
   743	  }
   744	
   745	  try {
   746	    fs.writeFileSync(marker_path, `${JSON.stringify({
   747	      pid: process.pid,
   748	      databasePath: target_path,
   749	      startedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
   750	    })}\n`, { mode: 0o600 });
   751	  } catch (_error: unknown) {
   752	    // Best-effort: marker failure must not block DB startup.
   753	  }
   754	}
   755	
   756	function remove_unclean_shutdown_marker(target_path: string): void {
   757	  const marker_path = get_unclean_shutdown_marker_path(target_path);
   758	  if (!marker_path) {
   759	    return;
   760	  }
   761	
   762	  try {
   763	    fs.rmSync(marker_path, { force: true });
   764	  } catch (_error: unknown) {
   765	    // Best-effort: marker cleanup must not block DB close.
   766	  }
   767	}

  1296	
  1297	  create_schema(new_db, { sqlite_vec_available: vec_available, get_embedding_dim });
  1298	  ensure_schema_version(new_db);
  1299	  drop_canonical_vector_payload_tables(new_db);
  1300	
  1301	  const dimCheck = validate_embedding_dimension_for_connection(new_db, vec_available);
  1302	  if (!dimCheck.valid && dimCheck.stored != null) {
  1303	    const msg = dimCheck.warning || `Dimension mismatch: DB=${dimCheck.stored}, provider=${dimCheck.current}`;
  1304	    console.error(`[vector-index] FATAL: ${msg}`);
  1305	    try { new_db.close(); } catch (_: unknown) { /* best-effort */ }
  1306	    throw new VectorIndexError(msg, VectorIndexErrorCode.INTEGRITY_ERROR);
  1307	  }
  1308	
  1309	  set_active_database_connection(new_db, target_path, vec_available);
  1310	
  1311	  // C1 FIX: Only cache in connection map after all validation passes
  1312	  db_connections.set(resolved_target, new_db);
  1313	
  1314	  return new_db;
  1315	}
  1316	
  1317	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  1318	   7. DATABASE UTILITIES
  1319	----------------------------------------------------------------*/
  1320	
  1321	/**
  1322	 * Closes the shared vector-index database connection.
  1323	 * @returns Nothing.
  1324	 */
  1325	export function close_db(): void {
  1326	  clear_prepared_statements();
  1327	  // C1 FIX: Close all tracked connections
  1328	  for (const [, conn] of db_connections) {
  1329	    try {
  1330	      if (conn !== db) {
  1331	        // Non-active tracked connections must also flush + TRUNCATE their
  1332	        // WAL before close, exactly like the active db below — otherwise a non-active connection
  1333	        // closes with only better-sqlite3's passive checkpoint and can leave un-checkpointed
  1334	        // frames that an abrupt later kill could corrupt (the corruption window).
  1335	        // Checkpoint BEFORE detaching the shard (the shard schema must still be attached).
  1336	        try { conn.pragma(`${ACTIVE_VECTOR_SCHEMA}.wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE)`); } catch (_: unknown) { /* best-effort: shard may not be attached on this conn */ }
  1337	        try { conn.pragma('wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE)'); } catch (_: unknown) { /* best-effort */ }
  1338	        detachActiveVectorShard(conn);
  1339	        conn.close();
  1340	      }
  1341	    } catch (_: unknown) { /* ignore close errors */ }
  1342	  }
  1343	  db_connections.clear();
  1344	  if (db) {
  1345	    const closing_db_path = db_path;
  1346	    // FTS-corruption prevention: flush + TRUNCATE the
  1347	    // WAL before close so context-index.sqlite is consistent at rest with an empty
  1348	    // WAL. better-sqlite3 `.close()` only does a passive checkpoint and can leave
  1349	    // un-checkpointed frames; an explicit TRUNCATE shrinks the window that an
  1350	    // abrupt later kill (e.g. SIGKILL on MCP reconnect) could corrupt — notably
  1351	    // FTS5 segment writes. Best-effort: a checkpoint failure must never block close.
  1352	    try { db.pragma(`${ACTIVE_VECTOR_SCHEMA}.wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE)`); } catch (_: unknown) { /* best-effort */ }
  1353	    let main_checkpoint_succeeded = false;
  1354	    try {
  1355	      db.pragma('wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE)');
  1356	      main_checkpoint_succeeded = true;
  1357	    } catch (_: unknown) { /* best-effort */ }
  1358	    // DR-011: The clean-shutdown marker semantic is "present == dirty" (it is written
  1359	    // on every open in initialize_db and removed only on a clean close). It must be
  1360	    // deleted ONLY after a confirmed-successful close. detachActiveVectorShard() and
  1361	    // db.close() can both throw; if the marker were removed before they ran (the prior
  1362	    // ordering) and one of them threw, the marker would be gone while the DB did NOT
  1363	    // close cleanly — so the next open would wrongly trust a dirty DB. Detach + close
  1364	    // first (if either throws we never reach the removal, so the marker survives), then
  1365	    // remove the marker inside the checkpoint-success guard.
  1366	    detachActiveVectorShard(db);
  1367	    db.close();
  1368	    if (main_checkpoint_succeeded) {
  1369	      remove_unclean_shutdown_marker(closing_db_path);
  1370	    }
  1371	    db = null;
  1372	  }
  1373	}
  1374

   346	function getUncleanShutdownMarkerPath(): string {
   347	  // Derive the marker dir from the ACTUAL opened DB path (vectorIndex.getDbPath()) — the same path the
   348	  // marker writer in vector-index-store uses — not the independently-derived DATABASE_PATH. Under a
   349	  // MEMORY_DB_PATH whose dirname differs from the resolved DB dir, DATABASE_PATH would point the boot check
   350	  // at the wrong dir and silently disable corruption detection. Falls back to
   351	  // DATABASE_PATH if the DB is not open yet (the boot check only runs post-connect, so getDbPath is set).
   352	  const dbPath = vectorIndex.getDbPath() || DATABASE_PATH;
   353	  return path.join(path.dirname(dbPath), UNCLEAN_SHUTDOWN_MARKER);
   354	}
   355	
   356	function getBootFtsIntegrityHealth(): BootFtsIntegrityHealth {
   357	  return bootFtsIntegrityHealth;
   358	}
   359	
   360	function runBootFtsIntegrityCheck(): void {
   361	  try {
   362	    vectorIndex.getDb()
   363	      .prepare("INSERT INTO memory_fts(memory_fts) VALUES('integrity-check')")
   364	      .run();
   365	    bootFtsIntegrityHealth = 'ok';
   366	  } catch (error: unknown) {
   367	    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error);
   368	    bootFtsIntegrityHealth = 'corrupt';
   369	    console.error([
   370	      '[context-server] ===== FTS5 SHADOW INDEX CORRUPTION DETECTED =====',
   371	      '[context-server] Boot marker indicates the previous mk-spec-memory shutdown was unclean.',
   372	      `[context-server] FTS5 integrity-check failed: ${message}`,
   373	      '[context-server] DETECT-ONLY: no DB recovery, index reconstruction, swap, or deletion was attempted.',
   374	      `[context-server] Runbook: ${FTS_CORRUPTION_RUNBOOK}`,
   375	      '[context-server] =================================================',
   376	    ].join('\n'));
   377	  }
   378	}
   379	
   380	function scheduleBootFtsIntegrityCheck(): void {
   381	  if (!fs.existsSync(getUncleanShutdownMarkerPath())) {
   382	    bootFtsIntegrityHealth = 'skipped';
   383	    return;
   384	  }

   389	export function maybeStructuralNudge(
   390	  task: string,
   391	  options: {
   392	    graphReady: boolean;
   393	    activationScaffoldReady: boolean;
   394	    surface?: StructuralRoutingNudge['surface'];
   395	  },
   396	): StructuralRoutingNudge | null {
   397	  const normalizedTask = task.trim();
   398	  if (!normalizedTask) {
   399	    return null;
   400	  }
   401	
   402	  if (!options.graphReady || !options.activationScaffoldReady) {
   403	    return null;
   404	  }
   405	
   406	  if (NON_STRUCTURAL_SUPPRESS_PATTERNS.some((pattern) => pattern.test(normalizedTask))) {
   407	    return null;
   408	  }
   409	
   410	  if (!STRUCTURAL_MISFIRE_PATTERNS.some((pattern) => pattern.test(normalizedTask))) {
   411	    return null;
   412	  }
   413	
   414	  return {
   415	    advisory: true,
   416	    readiness: 'ready',
   417	    preferredTool: 'mcp__mk_code_index__code_graph_query',
   418	    secondaryTool: 'mcp__mk_code_index__code_graph_context',
   419	    message: 'Advisory only: this looks like a structural question. Prefer `mcp__mk_code_index__code_graph_query` before Grep or Glob for callers, imports, outline, and dependency lookups.',
   420	    preservesAuthority: 'session_bootstrap',
   421	    surface: options.surface ?? 'response-hints',
   422	  };
   423	}
